Energy Recycling

What can be done with unused energy from large energy consumers? We answered this question by dealing hyper-efficiently with the residual heat that is emitted in the house. We redesigned the refrigerator to show and let people experience how this residual heat can be utilized.

Ai Compression

ExoSphere, an AI server that stores data and content.This replaces huge polluting data centers that facilitate cloud storage and services. The AI generates images, and films from the most necessary metadata. If everyone switches to ExoSphere, 70% of excisting data servers could be closed. This is an improvement for the environment.

Thirty Degrees

Ssueg, Ttal-Kkag, Ttok

Alternative visualisation towards reducing energy consumption in daily life. Our project interfaces revolve around (enticing)(inferring) on basic human psychological behavior of discontentment and satisfaction. We designed chargers that entice on the feeling of visual unease to stimulate the removal after usage. Moreover we designed a web-browser and smartphone interface that entices the removal of background applications and tabs after usage.

You don't need a blender

Blender is one of the most problematic appliances in modern kitchen in terms of energy consumption, thus we try to find alternative ways to blend food by basic manual tools in the kitchen. In the end, we designed an instruction to teach people to choose and use tools according to the food texture.

Memoirs of Hadera

Memoirs of hedera is a plant powered game that takes care of itself by informing the user of its need for attention. It imagines a world where taking care of our electricity source (plants) becomes a small amount of entertainment requiring human intervention. This game can only be played once every three days, can you keep it going?

the potential of the jansbeek

Our project highlights the potential value water power could provide. We do this in the city center of Arnhem. Water generators combined with simple components highlight the potential of blue power the Jansbeek or other streams in the world could supply. The future is set in water.

MORF

Introducing a change of consuming. The fashion industry has a huge energy footprint caused by overproduction and overconsumption. As long as the retailers are selling and the consumers are buying, everything’s fine right? The one suffering is the Earth. This Project is about changing consumerism and it’s consequences.
